\input{Integral-Compute-0044.HELP.tex}

\[
\int{{\frac{7 \, x^{2}}{\sqrt{-x^{2} - 18 \, x - 45}}}\;dx} = \answer{{-\frac{7}{2} \, \sqrt{-x^{2} - 18 \, x - 45} x + \frac{189}{2} \, \sqrt{-x^{2} - 18 \, x - 45} - 693 \, \arcsin\left(-\frac{1}{6} \, x - \frac{3}{2}\right)}+C}
\]
\end{problem}}%}

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Integration Compute Question 0044. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Compute the following integral:

\input{Integral-Compute-0044.HELP.tex}

\[
\int{{\frac{9 \, x^{2}}{\sqrt{x^{2} + 16 \, x + 55}}}\;dx} = \answer{{\frac{9}{2} \, \sqrt{x^{2} + 16 \, x + 55} x - 108 \, \sqrt{x^{2} + 16 \, x + 55} + \frac{1233}{2} \, \log\left(2 \, x + 2 \, \sqrt{x^{2} + 16 \, x + 55} + 16\right)}+C}
\]
\end{problem}}%}
